[Shortcut](/wiki/Wookieepedia:Shortcut "Wookieepedia:Shortcut"):  
WP:GA

Good articles on Wookieepedia

A Good article is an article that adheres to certain quality standards but cannot reach [Featured status](/wiki/Wookieepedia:Featured_articles "Wookieepedia:Featured articles") due to its limited content. At present, there are **3,635** Good articles, out of a total of 214,703 articles on Wookieepedia. Articles that no longer meet the criteria can be proposed for improvement or removal at the [Good article reviews](/wiki/Wookieepedia:Good_article_reviews "Wookieepedia:Good article reviews") page.

A small check mark ([![GA-Icon](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/GA-Icon.svg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/16?cb=20240801065847)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/GA-Icon.svg/revision/latest?cb=20240801065847)) in the top right corner of an article's page indicates that the article has achieved Good status.

[AgriCorps](/wiki/Wookieepedia:AgriCorps "Wookieepedia:AgriCorps"), see the [Canon](/wiki/Wookieepedia:Good_articles/Canon "Wookieepedia:Good articles/Canon"), [Legends](/wiki/Wookieepedia:Good_articles/Legends "Wookieepedia:Good articles/Legends"), and [OOU](/wiki/Wookieepedia:Good_articles/OOU "Wookieepedia:Good articles/OOU") subpages for listing purposes.

* [Legends](#)
